 These three new features will be in the notes issued by RBI: 1) Increasing size of numbers in the number panels
 The numbers in both the number panels of banknotes will be in increasing size from left to right
 isamen shuru ke teen akshar or ank alphanumeric aakaar main ek samaan honge
 In this new note, every number in the series will be in different sizes, if put it clearly, now all the numbers printed in the note will be in increasing order
 rigerv bank ke anusaar sankhya ko badhate hue kram main dene se aam log asli or nakli note main aasaani se fark kar sakegein
 Let us tell you that earlier the series numbers were the same
 2) ubhari blide line shurune noton main ubhari blide line shuru kii gai he jo note ke aage ke bhaag par daaen or baayen ore hogi
 In such a case, four lines are given in two blocks in a 100 rupee note
 500 rupee ke note main teen block (2-1-2) main paanch line di gai hai or vahiin 1,000 rupee ke note main chaar blokon (1-2-2-1) main chah line hongi

 3) Identification mark will be larger The size of the existing identification mark near the left end of the banknote has been increased

 ’inputah bhashaa People who are deficient in iron in their blood have a higher risk of dengue infection to others through mosquitoes
 ek adhyayan main yah daawa karte hue visheshgyon ne bataaya ki beemaari ke dauraan louh tatwon kaa seven karne vaale rogi machharon ke kaatane se hone vaale is rog ke prasar ko badhane se roak sakate hai
 Dengue fever is caused by the bite of Aedes mosquito of the Aedes aegypti species
 iske lakshanon main tej bukhaar, sharir par chakatte padana or tej dard hona shaamil hai
 In some cases of dengue, the patient is not treated at the right time leading to death
 vishwa swasthya sanghathan (WHO) ke anusaar har saal dengue ke kareeb 39 karod maamle aate hai or iskaa prakope ab africa, america, dakshin purv asia tathaa prashanth kshetra ke 100 se adhik deshon main he
 According to the study published in the journal Nature Microbiology, the dengue patients who have high levels of iron in their blood have less chance of further virus infection through blood sucking mosquitoes
 america ke connectikat vishvavidhyalay ke penghua wang ke netritv main anusandhankartaaon ne yah pataa lagane kaa prayaas kiya ki kya dengue rogi ke rakt kii gunvattta kaa dengue virus ke prasar par asar hota he
 They took blood samples of healthy workers and put dengue virus in every sample
 jab unhone machharon ko is rakt kaa seven karaayaa or dekha ki har batch main se kitne machhar sankramit hue hai to unhen parinaamon main kai antar dikhaai diye
 Wang and his colleagues found that this difference in results was associated with the amount of iron in the blood
 wang ne kaha, ‘‘khun main adhik louh tatv hone par kam sankhya main machhar sankramit hue
 Researchers obtained similar results by performing this experiment on mice
 unhone dekha ki raktaalpata se grast chuhon kaa rakt chusane vaale machharon ko virus kaa sankraman hone kii sambhaavna adhik thi
 The study team came to the conclusion that this is happening due to the mosquito repellent system
